            animation: fadeOut 0.5s ease-in forwards;
        }
        @keyframes fadeIn {
            from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(10px) scale(0.98); }
            to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0) scale(1); }
        }
        @keyframes fadeOut {
            from { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0) scale(1); }
            to { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(10px) scale(0.98); }

            color: inherit;
            opacity: 0.7;
        }
        .recite-flashcard {
            transition: transform 0.5s;

  { "id": 3998, "word": "当たる", "reading": "あたる", "meaning": "中奖", "level": "N4", "example": "ボールが頭に当たりました。", "example_meaning": "球打到头了。" },
  { "id": 3999, "word": "脱ぐ", "reading": "ぬぐ", "meaning": "脱", "level": "N4", "example": "家に入るとき、靴を脱ぎます。", "example_meaning": "进屋时脱鞋。" },
  { "id": 4000, "word": "親切な", "reading": "しんせつな", "meaning": "亲切的", "level": "N4", "example": "彼はとても親切な人です。", "example_meaning": "他是个非常亲切的人。" }

        ];

        const wordGrid = document.getElementById('word-grid');
        const searchBar = document.getElementById('search-bar');
        const levelFilters = document.getElementById('level-filters');
        const statusFilters = document.getElementById('status-filters');
        const modal = document.getElementById('word-modal');
        const modalContent = document.getElementById('modal-content');
        const closeModalBtn = document.getElementById('close-modal');
        const modalFooter = document.getElementById('modal-footer');
        const mainContent = document.getElementById('main-content');
        const startReciteBtn = document.getElementById('start-recite-btn');
        const reciteMode = document.getElementById('recite-mode');
        const exitReciteBtn = document.getElementById('exit-recite-btn');
        const reciteTimer = document.getElementById('recite-timer');
        const reciteProgress = document.getElementById('recite-progress');
        const flashcard = document.getElementById('recite-flashcard');
        const reciteWord = document.getElementById('recite-word');
        const reciteReading = document.getElementById('recite-reading');
        const reciteMeaning = document.getElementById('recite-meaning');
        const reciteExample = document.getElementById('recite-example');
        const revealBtn = document.getElementById('reveal-btn');
        const revealAction = document.getElementById('recite-reveal-action');
        const feedbackActions = document.getElementById('recite-feedback-actions');
        const knowBtn = document.getElementById('know-btn');
        const dontKnowBtn = document.getElementById('dont-know-btn');
        const certificateModal = document.getElementById('certificate-modal');
        const certificateCount = document.getElementById('certificate-count');
        const certificateDate = document.getElementById('certificate-date');
        const saveCertificateBtn = document.getElementById('save-certificate-btn');
        const retryReciteBtn = document.getElementById('retry-recite-btn');
        const closeCertificateBtn = document.getElementById('close-certificate-btn');

        let currentLevel = 'N5';
        let currentStatus = 'all';
        let searchTerm = '';
        let wordStatuses = {};
        let currentWordId = null;
        let reciteInterval;
        let reciteWords = [];
        let currentReciteIndex = 0;
        const RECITE_DURATION = 600;

        const loadStatuses = () => {
            const savedStatuses = localStorage.getItem('japaneseWordStatuses_v2');
            if (savedStatuses) {
                wordStatuses = JSON.parse(savedStatuses);
            } else {
                words.forEach(word => {
                    wordStatuses[word.id] = 'none';
                });
            }
        };

        const saveStatuses = () => {
            localStorage.setItem('japaneseWordStatuses_v2', JSON.stringify(wordStatuses));
        };

        const renderWords = () => {
            wordGrid.innerHTML = '';
            const filteredWords = words.filter(word => {
                const levelMatch = word.level === currentLevel;
                const statusMatch = currentStatus === 'all' || wordStatuses[word.id] === currentStatus;
                const searchMatch = word.word.includes(searchTerm) || word.reading.includes(searchTerm) || word.meaning.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase());
                return levelMatch && statusMatch && searchMatch;
            });
            
            if (filteredWords.length === 0) {
                wordGrid.innerHTML = `<p class="col-span-full text-center text-gray-500">在这片森林里，暂时没有找到呢...</p>`;
                return;
            }

            filteredWords.forEach(word => {
                const status = wordStatuses[word.id] || 'none';
                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = `word-card cursor-pointer p-4 shadow-sm flex flex-col justify-center items-center text-center bg-status-${status}`;
                card.dataset.id = word.id;
                card.innerHTML = `
                    <p class="text-2xl font-normal">${word.word}</p>
                    <p class="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">${word.reading}</p>
                `;
                card.addEventListener('click', () => openModal(word));
                wordGrid.appendChild(card);
            });
        };

        const updateFilterButtons = (filterGroup, currentFilter, dataAttribute) => {
            const buttons = filterGroup.querySelectorAll('button');
            const activeClasses = ['bg-[#A2B8C4]', 'text-white', 'border-[#A2B8C4]'];
            const inactiveClasses = ['bg-white', 'text-gray-700'];

            buttons.forEach(button => {
                if (button.dataset[dataAttribute] === currentFilter) {
                    button.classList.add(...activeClasses);
                    button.classList.remove(...inactiveClasses);
                } else {
                    button.classList.remove(...activeClasses);
                    button.classList.add(...inactiveClasses);
                }
            });
        };
        
        const openModal = (word) => {
            currentWordId = word.id;
            document.getElementById('modal-word').textContent = word.word;
            document.getElementById('modal-reading').textContent = word.reading;
            document.getElementById('modal-meaning').textContent = word.meaning;
            document.getElementById('modal-example').textContent = word.example;
            document.getElementById('modal-example-meaning').textContent = word.example_meaning;
            modal.classList.remove('hidden');
        };

        const closeModal = () => {
            modal.classList.add('hidden');
        };
        
        const startReciteSession = () => {
            mainContent.style.display = 'none';
            reciteMode.style.display = 'flex';
            
            const wordsForLevel = words.filter(w => w.level === currentLevel);
            if (wordsForLevel.length === 0) {
                alert('当前等级没有单词可供学习！');
                endReciteSession(true);
                return;
            }
            reciteWords = [...wordsForLevel].sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random());
            currentReciteIndex = 0;

            startTimer(RECITE_DURATION);
            displayReciteWord();
        };
        
        const endReciteSession = (immediate = false) => {
            clearInterval(reciteInterval);
            if (immediate) {
                reciteMode.style.display = 'none';
                mainContent.style.display = 'block';
                return;
            }
            reciteMode.style.display = 'none';
            mainContent.style.display = 'block';
            showCertificate();
        };

        const startTimer = (duration) => {
            let timer = duration;
            reciteTimer.textContent = '10:00';
            reciteProgress.textContent = `已复习 0 词`;
            reciteInterval = setInterval(() => {
                timer--;
                let minutes = parseInt(timer / 60, 10);
                let seconds = parseInt(timer % 60, 10);
                minutes = minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes;
                seconds = seconds < 10 ? "0" + seconds : seconds;
                reciteTimer.textContent = minutes + ":" + seconds;
                if (timer <= 0) {
                    endReciteSession();
                }
            }, 1000);
        };
        
        const displayReciteWord = () => {
            if (currentReciteIndex >= reciteWords.length) {
                currentReciteIndex = 0; // Loop
                reciteWords.sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random()); // Re-shuffle
            }
            
            flashcard.classList.remove('is-flipped');
            revealAction.classList.remove('hidden');
            feedbackActions.classList.add('hidden');
            
            const word = reciteWords[currentReciteIndex];
            reciteWord.textContent = word.word;
            reciteReading.textContent = word.reading;
            reciteMeaning.textContent = word.meaning;
            reciteExample.textContent = word.example;
            
            reciteProgress.textContent = `已复习 ${currentReciteIndex} 词`;
        };
        
        const nextReciteWord = () => {
            currentReciteIndex++;
            setTimeout(displayReciteWord, 300);
        };

        const showCertificate = () => {
            certificateCount.textContent = currentReciteIndex;
            const today = new Date();
            certificateDate.textContent = `${today.getFullYear()}年${today.getMonth() + 1}月${today.getDate()}日`;
            certificateModal.classList.remove('hidden');
        };

        searchBar.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            searchTerm = e.target.value;
            renderWords();
        });

        levelFilters.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.tagName === 'BUTTON') {
                currentLevel = e.target.dataset.level;
                updateFilterButtons(levelFilters, currentLevel, 'level');
                renderWords();
            }
        });
        
        statusFilters.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
             if (e.target.tagName === 'BUTTON') {
                currentStatus = e.target.dataset.status;
                updateFilterButtons(statusFilters, currentStatus, 'status');
                renderWords();
            }
        });

        closeModalBtn.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
        modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.id === 'word-modal') closeModal();
        });

        modalFooter.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.tagName === 'BUTTON') {
                const newStatus = e.target.dataset.status;
                if (currentWordId !== null) {
                    wordStatuses[currentWordId] = newStatus;
                    saveStatuses();
                    renderWords();
                    closeModal();
                }
            }
        });

        startReciteBtn.addEventListener('click', startReciteSession);
        exitReciteBtn.addEventListener('click', () => endReciteSession(true));

        revealBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            flashcard.classList.add('is-flipped');
            revealAction.classList.add('hidden');
            feedbackActions.classList.remove('hidden');
        });
        
        knowBtn.addEventListener('click', () => nextReciteWord());
        dontKnowBtn.addEventListener('click', () => nextReciteWord());

        saveCertificateBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const cardToCapture = document.getElementById('certificate-card');
            if (cardToCapture) {
                html2canvas(cardToCapture).then(canvas => {
                    const link = document.createElement('a');
                    link.download = '言叶の森-学习证明.png';
                    link.href = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
                    link.click();
                });
            }
        });

        retryReciteBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            certificateModal.classList.add('hidden');
            startReciteSession();
        });
        
        closeCertificateBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            certificateModal.classList.add('hidden');
        });

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            loadStatuses();
            updateFilterButtons(levelFilters, currentLevel, 'level');
            updateFilterButtons(statusFilters, currentStatus, 'status');
            renderWords();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
